## Embedded A4 Reference Tables

The inventory below is embedded verbatim from the a4 renames spec and serves as the self-contained executor source for this plan.

## 036 A2 Renames

This file is the cleaned Phase 036 execution surface for the a2 rename inventory.
It keeps only the rows that were rechecked against the current workspace and
replaces archived suggestions with the live signatures that exist today.

The archived `036-a2-renames-old.md` file remains the historical snapshot.
Use this file for current planning and treat the historical alias column as
traceability only.

## Verification Rules

- Use the `Current Signature` column as the authority for planning and follow-up.
- Keep the `Historical Alias` column only as archive context.
- Recheck the file path and line number against the live workspace before any
  follow-up rename or documentation task.
- If a symbol appears in multiple files, each row is independent and must be
  verified against its own path.
- Do not infer a current signature from a prefix match alone.
